province_event = { # Coal Found
    id = 199035
    title = "EVTNAME199036"
    desc = "EVTDESC199036"

    trigger = {
        owned_by = THIS
        controlled_by = THIS
        owner = {
            OR = {
                civilized = yes
                tag = KOR

            }
        }

            province_id = 1664  #Kumamoto, Japan

                }
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1860
				OR = {
                    province_id = 1124  #Qazvin
					province_id = 2282  #Loja

					province_id = 3648	#Hamilton #https://csegrecorder.com/articles/view/assessing-risk-to-the-ermelo-ring-road-from-historical-coal-undermining
				}
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1850
                OR = {
					province_id = 2329 #Araucania #https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lota,_Chile
                    province_id = 221  #Hagerstown

					province_id = 765 #Caller
                }
            }
			AND = {
				year = 1852
				province_id = 745 #Livorno #https://it.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ferrovia_di_Monterufoli
			}
			AND = {
				year = 1900
				OR = {
					province_id = 1399	#Palembang (Bukit Asam)
					province_id = 391	#Hasselt #https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Campine
					province_id = 449	#Leipzig #https://www.industriedenkmal-stiftung.de/en/monuments/zeche-sterkrade
				}
				NOT = { trade_goods = oil }
			}
        }
        NOT = {
			trade_goods = coal
			trade_goods = gold
			trade_goods = gems
		}
        NOT = { has_province_modifier = switched_production }

        owner = {
            war = no
            OR = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    trade_goods = coal
                    NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                }
                any_neighbor_country = {
                    war = no
                    any_owned_province = {
                        trade_goods = coal
                        NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                    }
                }
                any_greater_power = {
                    war = no
                    any_owned_province = {
                        trade_goods = coal
                        NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    allow_multiple_instances = no

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        months = 40
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1880
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1890
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1900
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1905
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 2
            owner = { civilized = no }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = "EVTOPTA199035"
        trade_goods = coal
        add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
        ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }
    option = {
        name = "EVT199034OPTB"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}

			}
			AND = {
				province_id = 2169 #Colima #https://www.researchgate.net/figure/Figura-1-Mapa-de-localizacion-del-yacimiento-de-Pena-Colorada-ESTUDIOS-PREVIOS-Y_fig1_273439003
				year = 1914

                    war = no
                    any_owned_province = {
                        trade_goods = iron
                        NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.05 type = labourers } }

                }
            }
        }
    }

    allow_multiple_instances = no

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        months = 40
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.75
            year = 1910
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1915
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.5
            year = 1920
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = "EVTOPTA199035"
        trade_goods = iron
		remove_province_modifier = silver_mine
        add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
        owner = {
            random_owned = {
                limit = { province_id = 1631 NOT = { trade_goods = silk } } #Wonju
                trade_goods = silk
                add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { province_id = 1624 NOT = { trade_goods = tea } } #Hanseong
                trade_goods = tea
                add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
            }
            random_owned = {
                limit = { province_id = 1636 NOT = { trade_goods = tea } } #Taejon
                trade_goods = tea
                add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
            }
        }
        ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }
    option = {
        name = "EVT199034OPTB"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}
province_event = { # Sulfur Found
    id = 199075
    title = "EVTNAME199075"
    desc = "EVTDESC199075"

    trigger = {
        owned_by = THIS
        controlled_by = THIS
        OR = {
            AND = {
                year = 1842
				province_id = 561 #Weimar
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1850
				province_id = 2561 #Siegburg
            }
			AND = {
				year = 1851
				province_id = 555 #Dessau
			}
            AND = {
                year = 1865
				province_id = 85 #Sonoma
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1867
				NOT = { year = 1886 } #Charleston Earthquake
				province_id = 205 #Charleston
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1872
				province_id = 311 #Skien
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1883
				province_id = 199 #St Augustine
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1885
				province_id = 1727 #Gafsa
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1893
				province_id = 3256 #Sondershausen
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1895
				province_id = 562 #Gotha
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1901
				province_id = 554 #Erfurt
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1902
				province_id = 3647 #Victoria
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1903
				province_id = 141 #Lake Charles
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1904
				province_id = 410 #Colmar
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1910
				province_id = 3906 #Rudolstadt
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1925
				OR = {
					province_id = 983 #Kandalaksha
					province_id = 3658 #Solikamsk
				}
            }
            AND = {
                year = 1931
				province_id = 2563 #Asfi
            }
        }
        NOT = {
			trade_goods = sulphur
		}
        NOT = { has_province_modifier = switched_production }

        owner = {
            war = no
            OR = {
                any_owned_province = {
                    trade_goods = sulphur
                    NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                }
                any_neighbor_country = {
                    war = no
                    any_owned_province = {
                        trade_goods = sulphur
                        NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                    }
                }
                any_greater_power = {
                    war = no
                    any_owned_province = {
                        trade_goods = sulphur
                        NOT = { unemployment_by_type = { value = 0.01 type = labourers } }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    allow_multiple_instances = no

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "EVTOPTA199035"
        trade_goods = sulphur
        add_province_modifier = { name = switched_production duration = 365 }
        ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }
    option = {
        name = "EVT199034OPTB"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}

province_event = {
    id = 199018
    title = "EVTNAME199015" #Cash Crops - Wool
    desc = "EVTDESC199018"

    trigger = {
        owned_by = THIS
        controlled_by = THIS
        province_control_days = 1095
        owner = {
            war = no
            civilized = yes
        }
        NOT = {
            trade_goods = wool
            has_province_modifier = switched_production
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                unemployment_by_type = { type = farmers value = 0.5 }
                has_pop_type = farmers
                work_available = { worker = farmers }
            }
            AND = {
                unemployment_by_type = { type = labourers value = 0.5 }
                has_pop_type = labourers
                work_available = { worker = labourers }
            }
        }
        OR = {
            terrain = plains
            terrain = savanna
            terrain = dryhills
            terrain = steppe
            terrain = hills
        }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        months = 4000
        modifier = {
            factor = 0.001
            NOT = { trade_goods = cotton }
            NOT = { trade_goods = dye }
            NOT = { trade_goods = wool }
            NOT = { trade_goods = silk }
            NOT = { trade_goods = coal }
            NOT = { trade_goods = sulphur }
            NOT = { trade_goods = iron }
            NOT = { trade_goods = timber }
            NOT = { trade_goods = tropical_wood }
            NOT = { trade_goods = rubber }
            NOT = { trade_goods = oil }
            NOT = { trade_goods = precious_metal }
            NOT = { trade_goods = precious_goods } NOT = { trade_goods = ivory } NOT = { trade_goods = slave_trading } NOT = { trade_goods = mercury }
            NOT = { trade_goods = gems } NOT = { trade_goods = pearls } NOT = { trade_goods = gold }
            NOT = { trade_goods = cattle }
            NOT = { trade_goods = fish }
            NOT = { trade_goods = fruit }
            NOT = { trade_goods = grain }
            NOT = { trade_goods = tobacco } NOT = { trade_goods = sugar }
            NOT = { trade_goods = tea }
            NOT = { trade_goods = coffee }
            NOT = { trade_goods = opium }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = "EVT199022OPTA"
        trade_goods = wool
        add_province_modifier = {
            name = switched_production
            duration = 1825
        }
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
    }

    option = {
        name = "EVT199034OPTB"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
    }
}

province_event = {
    id = 199019
    title = "EVTNAME199015" #Cash Crops - Fruit
    desc = "EVTDESC199019"

    trigger = {
        owned_by = THIS
        controlled_by = THIS
        province_control_days = 1095
        owner = {
            war = no
            civilized = yes
        }
        NOT = {
            trade_goods = fruit
            has_province_modifier = switched_production
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                unemployment_by_type = { type = farmers value = 0.5 }
                has_pop_type = farmers
                work_available = { worker = farmers }
            }
            AND = {
                unemployment_by_type = { type = labourers value = 0.5 }

                work_available = { worker = labourers }
            }

        OR = {
            terrain = farmlands

            terrain = new_world_jungle
            terrain = jungle_farmland
            terrain = jungle_hills

    }

        months = 2000

            factor = 0.001
            NOT = { trade_goods = cotton }
            NOT = { trade_goods = dye }
            NOT = { trade_goods = wool }

            NOT = { trade_goods = tropical_wood }
            NOT = { trade_goods = rubber }
            NOT = { trade_goods = oil }
            NOT = { trade_goods = precious_metal }
            NOT = { trade_goods = precious_goods } NOT = { trade_goods = ivory } NOT = { trade_goods = slave_trading } NOT = { trade_goods = mercury }
            NOT = { trade_goods = gems } NOT = { trade_goods = pearls } NOT = { trade_goods = gold }

            NOT = { trade_goods = fruit }

            NOT = { trade_goods = tea }

province_event = {
    id = 199030
    title = "EVTNAME199030" #Fisheries in $PROVINCENAME$
    desc = "EVTDESC199030"

    trigger = {
        owned_by = THIS
        controlled_by = THIS
        province_control_days = 1095
        owner = {
            war = no
            civilized = yes
        }
        NOT = {
            trade_goods = fish

			clr_country_flag = theravada_country

			clr_country_flag = protestant_country
			clr_country_flag = mormon_country

			clr_country_flag = mahayana_country

			clr_country_flag = theravada_country

			clr_country_flag = sikh_country
			clr_country_flag = animist_country
			add_accepted_culture = herero
			add_accepted_culture = chokwe
			add_accepted_culture = ovimbundu
		}

		ANG = { all_core = { remove_core = ANG } }
		2000 = { add_core = ANG }
		POR_2003 = { add_core = ANG }
		POR_2006 = { add_core = ANG }
		POR_1999 = { add_core = ANG }
		POR_2004 = { add_core = ANG }

				}

		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = shinto_country } } ANG = { religion = shinto set_country_flag = shinto_country } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = mahayana_country } } ANG = { religion = mahayana set_country_flag = mahayana_country } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = gelugpa_country } } ANG = { religion = gelugpa set_country_flag = gelugpa_country } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = theravada_country } } ANG = { religion = theravada set_country_flag = theravada_country } }

		BKF = {
			clr_country_flag = sunni_country
